## muc

`muc~~h0_02_sec_2`


**1a)** — desid.
 1) *mumukṣati, ˚te*
 a) act. frei zu machen im Begriff stehen: *mumukṣati vatsaṃ kṛṣṇaḥ*
[P. 7,4,57](https://ashtadhyayi.com/sutraani/7/4/57), Sch.
fahren zu lassen —, aufzugeben im Begriff stehen: *prāṇānkasmānmumukṣasi*
[KATHĀS. 73,18.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/kss/index.html?73,18) zu schleudern im Begriff stehen: *vajraṃ mumukṣanniva vajrapāṇiḥ*
[RAGH. 2,42.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/raghuvamsa/app1?2,42)

- **RU:** — desid.

## muc (paryA+)

`muc~~h0_10_pary_a`


**1)** — *paryā* rund herum ablösen und abnehmen: *ghaṭaṃ paryāmuñcati* (von der Töpferscheibe)
[GAUḌAP.] zu [SĀṂKHYAK. 67.]

- **RU:** — *paryā* снимать по кругу, отделять и снимать: *ghaṭaṃ paryāmuñcati* (с гончарного круга)
[GAUḌAP.] к [SĀṂKHYAK. 67.]
- **EN:** — *paryā* "to detach all around and take off": *ghaṭaṃ paryāmuñcati* (from the potter's wheel)
[GAUḌAP.] to [SĀṂKHYAK. 67.]
  <sub>DCS 3914 · attested</sub>

**1)** — *abhinis*, partic. *abhinirmukta*
[M. 2,221.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/manu/index.html?2,221)
[AK. 2,7,54.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/amara_dlc/app1?2,7,54)
[H. 860.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/abch2/app1?860)
[KULL.] zu [M. 2,220](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/manu/index.html?2,220) fehlerhaft für *abhinimrukta* .
- **EN:** — *abhinis*, partic. *abhinirmukta*
[M. 2,221.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/manu/index.html?2,221)
[AK. 2,7,54.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/amara_dlc/app1?2,7,54)
[H. 860.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/abch2/app1?860)

## vi-nis-muc

`muc~~h0_17_vinis`


**1)** — *vinis*
 1) pass. sich losmachen, sich befreien von: *yathā pādodarastvacā vinirmucyate*
[PRAŚNOP. 5,5.] *ye tu tatra vinirmuktāḥ sārthātkecidavikṣatāḥ* so v. a. mit heiler Haut davongekommen *(sārthāt* gehört zu *ye)*
[MBH. 3,2552.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/mbhcalc?3.2552) *brahmatejovinirmukta* glücklich entkommen
[BHĀG. P. 1,8,17.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/bhagp_bur/app1/?1,8,17) *doṣaiḥ* frei von
[SUŚR. 1,26,3.] *sarvebhyo 'pi vinirmuktaṃ kuru (mām)*
[PAÑCAR. 2,4,18.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/pancar/app1?2,4,18) *sarvadvaṃdva˚*
[M. 6,81.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/manu/index.html?6,81) *janmabandha˚*
[BHAG. 2,51.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/bhagavadgita/app1?2,51) *sarvavyādhi˚*
[MBH. 3,6027.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/mbhcalc?3.6027) *meghalekhā˚ (śaśimaṇḍala)*
[4,498.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/mbhcalc?4.498) [13,878.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/mbhcalc?13.878) [KATHĀS. 16,105.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/kss/index.html?16,105) [VARĀH. BṚH. S. 48,87.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/brihatsam/app1?48,87) [55,1.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/brihatsam/app1?55,1) [NĪLAK. 40.] [Verz. d. Oxf. H. 20,a,8](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/Oxf_Cat_Aufrecht/index.html?20) v. u. [P. 3,4,77](https://ashtadhyayi.com/sutraani/3/4/77), Sch.
- **EN:** — *vinis*
 1) pass. to free oneself, to disengage oneself from: *yathā pādodarastvacā vinirmucyate*
[PRAŚNOP. 5,5.] *ye tu tatra vinirmuktāḥ sārthātkecidavikṣatāḥ* so v. a. escaped unscathed *(sārthāt* belongs to *ye)*
[MBH. 3,2552.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/mbhcalc?3.2552) *brahmatejovinirmukta* escaped happily
[BHĀG. P. 1,8,17.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/bhagp_bur/app1/?1,8,17) *doṣaiḥ* free from
[SUŚR. 1,26,3.] *sarvebhyo 'pi vinirmuktaṃ kuru (mām)*
[PAÑCAR. 2,4,18.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/pancar/app1?2,4,18) *sarvadvaṃdva˚*
[M. 6,81.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/manu/index.html?6,81) *janmabandha˚*
[BHAG. 2,51.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/bhagavadgita/app1?2,51) *sarvavyādhi˚*
[MBH. 3,6027.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/mbhcalc?3.6027) *meghalekhā˚ (śaśimaṇḍala)*
[4,498.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/mbhcalc?4.498) [13,878.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/mbhcalc?13.878) [KATHĀS. 16,105.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/kss/index.html?16,105) [VARĀH. BṚH. S. 48,87.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/brihatsam/app1?48,87) [55,1.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/brihatsam/app1?55,1) [NĪLAK. 40.] [Verz. d. Oxf. H. 20,a,8](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/Oxf_Cat_Aufrecht/index.html?20) v. u. [P. 3,4,77](https://ashtadhyayi.com/sutraani/3/4/77), Sch.

**2)** — 2) fahren lassen, aufgeben: *vinirmucya kalevaram*
[HARIV. 6488.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/hariv?6488)
- **EN:** — 2) to let go, to give up: *vinirmucya kalevaram*
[HARIV. 6488.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/hariv?6488)

**3)** — 3) schleudern: *rāmacāpavinirmuktaiḥ sāyakaiḥ*

[4,15,22.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/ramayanagorr/?4,15,22)
- **EN:** — 3) to hurl: *rāmacāpavinirmuktaiḥ sāyakaiḥ*
[R. 3,31,22.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/ramayanagorr/?3,31,22) *(muṣṭiḥ) yaste mūrdhni vinirmuktaḥ prāṇānapahariṣyati*

## pari-muc

`muc~~h0_18_pari`


**1)** — *pari*
 1) lösen, ablösen, abnehmen: *puruṣaṃ parimuktabandhanaṃ karoti*
[ŚĀK. 75,10.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/shakuntala/app2?75,10) *tathā saṃnahanānyeṣāṃ parimucya samantataḥ* (von einem Baume)
[MBH. 4,1320.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/mbhcalc?4.1320) befreien: *muñcāmi tvā vaiśvānarādarṇavānmahataspari*
[AV. 1,10,4.](https://sanskrit-lexicon.github.io/avlinks/avhymns/av01.010.html#av01.010.04) med. pass. sich ablösen —, sich befreien von: *śvātreṇa yatpitrormucyase pari*
[ṚV. 1,31,4.](https://sanskrit-lexicon.github.io/rvlinks/rvhymns/rv01.031.html#rv01.031.04) *śoṇāśvāḥ paryamucyanta rathabandhāt*
[MBH. 7,8787.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/mbhcalc?7.8787) *kaluṣeṇādya mahatā medinī parimucyatām*
[R. 2,97,27](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/ramayanaschl/?2,97,27) ([106,24](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/ramayanagorr/?2,106,24) [GORR.]). *pāpebhyaḥ parimucyate*
[MBH. 13,5551.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/mbhcalc?13.5551) *kaṣṭātsaṃsārāt*
[14,455.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/mbhcalc?14.455) *ṛṣidevamanuṣyāṇāṃ* (sc. *ṛṇāt) parimukto 'smi dharmataḥ*
[1,4659.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/mbhcalc?1.4659) *meghoparodhaparimuktaśaśāṅkavaktrā*
[ṚT. 3,7.] *rāhūparāgaparimuktamivendubimbam*
[CAURAP. 10.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/bhartrhari/app1?10) frei —, erlöst werden (von

den Banden der Welt)
[KAUŚ. 139.]
[MAITRYUP. 6,34.] *parimucyanti sarve*
[MUṆḌ. UP. 3,2,6.]

- **RU:** — *pari*
 1) развязывать, отвязывать, снимать: *puruṣaṃ parimuktabandhanaṃ karoti*
[ŚĀK. 75,10.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/shakuntala/app2?75,10) *tathā saṃnahanānyeṣāṃ parimucya samantataḥ* (с дерева)
[MBH. 4,1320.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/mbhcalc?4.1320) освобождать: *muñcāmi tvā vaiśvānarādarṇavānmahataspari*

[ṚV. 1,31,4.](https://sanskrit-lexicon.github.io/rvlinks/rvhymns/rv01.031.html#rv01.031.04) *śoṇāśvāḥ paryamucyanta rathabandhāt*

[KATHĀS. 29,45.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/kss/index.html?29,45) — desid. s. *parimokṣa* .

- **RU:** — 2) покидать, оставлять, отпускать: *dvijātīn — na śaśāka — parimoktuṃ rathena saḥ* так v. a. расставаться с
[R. 2,45,19.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/ramayanaschl/?2,45,19) *parimucya tām (tarim)*
[PRAB. 102,15.] *parimuktasaṅga*
[BHĀG. P. 2,7,10.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/bhagp_bur/app1/?2,7,10) pass. в том же Bed., вероятно, ошибочно: *yaścāgnīnparimucyeta* так v. a. пренебрегать
[MBH. 12,1213.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/mbhcalc?12.1213) *yaścāgnīnapavidhyeta* [ed. Bomb.] отпускать, отдавать от себя: *tejomayaṃ tu yadyantraṃ tajjvālāḥ parimuñcati*
[KATHĀS. 29,45.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/kss/index.html?29,45) — desid. s. *parimokṣa* .

[MBH. 12,1213.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/mbhcalc?12.1213) *yaścāgnīnapavidhyeta* [ed. Bomb.] to dismiss, to let go of: *tejomayaṃ tu yadyantraṃ tajjvālāḥ parimuñcati*

**2)** — 2) Jmd freilassen, entlassen: *mahākratoramuṃ turaṃgaṃ pratimoktumarhasi*

[MṚCCH. 116,10.] *prāptamarthaṃ tu yo māhocchāntvanaiḥ pratimuñcati*

- **EN:** — *vi* to unfasten, untie, free; med. to unfasten something for oneself or on one's own account, z. B. to unharness one's own (horses): *vi mumoktu pāśān*

**3)** — 3〉 ablösen, abbinden, lösen. *kaṇṭham* die Kehle lösen, so v. a. seine Stimme erheben. *prāṇān* Jmds (Gen.) Lebensgeister lösen, so v. a. Jmd das Leben nehmen. *mukta* losgebunden; abgelöst, herabgefallen (Frucht); aufgelöst, so v. a. erschlafft (die Glieder des Körpers).

- **EN:** — 3) to detach, untie, loosen. *kaṇṭham* "to loosen the throat," i.e. v. a. to raise one's voice. *prāṇān* "to loosen someone's (Gen.) vital spirits," i.e. v. a. to take someone's life. *mukta* untied; detached, fallen off (of fruit); relaxed, i.e. v. a. slackened (of the limbs of the body).

## muc

`muc~~h0_zz_pw02`


**1)** — 1〉 _Adj._ am Ende eines Comp.

- **RU:** — 1〉 _Adj._ в конце Comp.
- **EN:** **2.** *muc*
— 1) _Adj._ at the end of a Comp.
  <sub>DCS 3914 · attested</sub>

**1a)** — a〉 befreiend von.

- **RU:** — a〉 освобождающий от.
- **EN:** — a) freeing from, liberating from.
  <sub>DCS 3914 · attested</sub>

**1b)** — b〉 entlassend, von sich gebend, ausströmend.

- **RU:** — b〉 испускающий, изливающий, выпускающий.
- **EN:** — b) discharging, giving forth, emitting, pouring out.
  <sub>DCS 3914 · attested</sub>

**1c)** — c〉 schleudernd.

- **RU:** — c〉 мечущий, пускающий.
- **EN:** — c) hurling, casting, flinging.
  <sub>DCS 3914 · attested</sub>

- **RU:** — 2〉 _f._ освобождение в *āmuc*.
- **EN:** — 2) _f._ liberation, release, in *āmuc*.
  <sub>DCS 3914 · attested</sub>
